      :ARG0 (c / country :name (n / name :op1 "France"))
      :ARG1 (a / and
            :op1 (a2 / ally-01
                  :ARG1 (a3 / and
                        :op1 c
                        :op2 c2)
                  :ARG3 (c3 / country :name (n3 / name :op1 "Germany")))
            :op2 (d / demilitarize-01
                  :ARG1 (a4 / and
                        :op1 c
                        :op2 c2)
                  :ARG2 (s / sea :name (n4 / name :op1 "English" :op2 "Channel"))))
      :ARG3 (c2 / country :name (n2 / name :op1 "England")))

# ::id dip_validation_0020.2
# ::snt England send to France that Hello France, England too am interested in moving east with France and England think a channel DMZ is a great idea.     England'll be doing a fairly standard English opening so let's see how russia and germany open to plan tactics next season.
(a / agree-01
      :ARG0 (c / country :name (n / name :op1 "England"))
      :ARG1 (a2 / and
            :op1 (a3 / ally-01
                  :ARG1 (a4 / and
                        :op1 c
                        :op2 c2)
                  :ARG3 (c3 / country :name (n3 / name :op1 "Germany")))
            :op2 (d / demilitarize-01
                  :ARG1 (a5 / and
                        :op1 c
                        :op2 c2)
                  :ARG2 (s / sea :name (n4 / name :op1 "English" :op2 "Channel"))))
      :ARG2 (c2 / country :name (n2 / name :op1 "France")))

# ::id dip_validation_0020.3
# ::snt France send to England that England Sounds good
(a / agree-01
      :ARG0 (c / country :name (n / name :op1 "France"))
      :ARG2 (c2 / country :name (n2 / name :op1 "England")))

# ::id dip_validation_0020.4
# ::snt France send to England that England France is going to do a standard opening too, MAO, Spain, and burgundy
(m / move-01
      :ARG1 (f / fleet
            :mod (c / country :name (n / name :op1 "France")))
      :ARG2 (a / and
            :op1 (s / sea :name (n2 / name :op1 "Mid-Atlantic" :op2 "Ocean"))
            :op2 (p / province :name (n3 / name :op1 "Spain"))
            :op3 (p2 / province :name (n4 / name :op1 "Burgundy"))))

# ::id dip_validation_0020.5
# ::snt England send to France that Do France want to Stab out the gate? Interesting tactics.
(b / betray-01
      :ARG0 (c / country :name (n / name :op1 "France"))
      :ARG1 (c2 / country :name (n2 / name :op1 "England")))

# ::id dip_validation_0020.6
# ::snt France send to England that Haha, sorry. Maybe France and England can work together sometime in the future(if England were willing to trust France  ). Good luck though.
(b / betray-01

      :ARG1 (c2 / country :name (n2 / name :op1 "England")))

# ::id dip_validation_0020.7
# ::snt France send to England that Ok, France didn't think Germany would betray France but they did. No matter what situation England's in, France and England have to all start working together to stop Germany or they will win.
(a / and
      :op1 (b / betray-01
            :ARG0 (c / country :name (n / name :op1 "Germany"))
            :ARG1 (c2 / country :name (n2 / name :op1 "France")))
      :op2 (p / propose-01
            :ARG0 c2
            :ARG1 (a2 / ally-01
                  :ARG1 (a3 / and
                        :op1 c2
                        :op2 c3
                        :op3 (c4 / country :name (n4 / name :op1 "Italy"))
                        :op4 (c5 / country :name (n5 / name :op1 "Russia"))
                        :op5 (c6 / country :name (n6 / name :op1 "Austria")))
                  :ARG3 c)
            :ARG3 (c3 / country :name (n3 / name :op1 "England"))))

# ::id dip_validation_0020.10
# ::snt England send to France that how do France feel about supporting England into the north sea?
(p / propose-01
      :ARG0 (c / country :name (n / name :op1 "England"))
      :ARG1 (s / support-01
            :ARG0 c2
            :ARG1 (m / move-01
                  :ARG1 (f / fleet
                        :mod c)
                  :ARG2 (s2 / sea :name (n3 / name :op1 "North" :op2 "Sea"))))
      :ARG3 (c2 / country :name (n2 / name :op1 "France")))

# ::id dip_validation_0020.11
# ::snt France send to England that England will do, with both fleets.
(a / agree-01
      :ARG0 (c / country :name (n / name :op1 "France"))
      :ARG1 (s / support-01
            :ARG0 c
            :ARG1 (m / move-01
                  :ARG1 (f / fleet
                        :mod c2)
                  :ARG2 (s2 / sea :name (n3 / name :op1 "North" :op2 "Sea")))
            :instrument (f2 / fleet :quant 2
                  :mod c))
      :ARG2 (c2 / country :name (n2 / name :op1 "England")))
